------------------------

Why is it called Arafah?

'Ata'a Ibn Rabah (rahimahullah d. 115 AH) said: It was termed "Arafah" because angel Jibreel (alaihisalam ) used to show Ibraheem (alaihisalam) the rites (of the pilgrimage). And he (Jibreel) would ask, "Arafata?" "Arafata?" "Did you understand?" "Did you understand?" So it was named "Arafah"

[Musannaf Ibn Abi Shaybah (rahimahullah) 14131].

04/06/2025, 11:22 am - Muzammil New: Yes 

Masāil al-Imām Aḥmad with riwāyah of his son 'Abdullah 912

He acted upon the Ḥadīth narrated marfū'an with Ḥasan Isnād in al-Bazzār 3922 and mawqūfan with Ḥasan Isnād in Shu'ab al-Īmān 165; Usāmah bin Zayd al-Laythī is authenticated by majority 

Ibn Ḥajar, al-Sakhawi and shaykh Amanpuri authenticated first one in his book of tawassul

Second one by shaykh Sa'd al-Shithri and he defended the claim that this could be from the isrāīlīyāt

This has no evidence for calling upon Angels or the Jinn as this is a specific case where the Prophet ﷺ himself told us they are present and have the ability to help us when we get lost

In other cases we don't even know if they're present or able so that will be shirk without a doubt

06/06/2025, 2:50 am - Muzammil New: *Sunan of 'Eid*
________________________________

Muḥammad bin Isḥāq (bin Yasār) said: I said to Nāfiʿ: “What would Ibn ʿUmar do on the day of ʿĪd?” He said: *“He would attend ṣalāt al-Fajr with the Imām, then he would return to his house and perform his ghusl like his ghusl for janābah (major impurity), and he would wear his best clothes and perfume himself with the best (fragrance) he had. Then he would go out until he reached the Muṣallā (ʿĪd prayer ground) and sit in it until the Imām came. When the Imām came, he would pray with him, then he would return and enter the Masjid of the Prophet ﷺ and pray two rakʿahs in it, then he would come to his house.”*

_[Musnad al-Ḥārith (207); Isnād Ḥasan]_

محمد بن إسحاق قال: قلت لنافع: كيف كان ‌ابن ‌عمر يصنع يوم ‌العيد؟ قال: كان يشهد صلاة الفجر مع الإمام ثم يرجع إلى بيته فيغتسل غسله من الجنابة ويلبس أحسن ثيابه ويتطيب بأطيب ما عنده ثم يخرج حتى يأتي المصلى فيجلس فيه حتى يجيء الإمام ، فإذا جاء الإمام صلى معه ثم يرجع فيدخل مسجد النبي صلى الله عليه وسلم فيصلي فيه ركعتين ثم يأتي بيته

_[مسند الحارث (٢٠٧) وسنده حسن]_

From Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both), he said: "Indeed, Allāh, the Mighty and Majestic, has angels other than the Ḥafaẓah (Guardian Angels) who write down what falls from the leaves of trees. [Shuʿab al-Īmān (165); Isnād Ḥasan]

*Ibn 'Umar (may Allāh be pleased with them both) used to say Takbīr in Minā during the days (of Tashrīq), and after the prayers, and on his bed, and in the prayers, and in his tent, and in his gathering, and while walking, throughout all those days.*

_[Akhbār Makkah by al-Fākihī (2583) and al-Awsat by Ibn al-Mundhir (2190); Jayyid asānīd ]_


ابن عمر رضي الله عنهما كان يكبّر بمنى تلك الأيام، ‌وخلف ‌الصلوات، ‌وعلى ‌فراشه، وفي الصلوات، وفي فسطاطه، وفي مجلسه، وفي ممشاه تلك الأيام جميعا.

_[أخبار مكة للفاكهي (٢٥٨٤) والأوسط لابن المنذر (٢١٩٠) وسندهما جيد]_
06/06/2025, 6:50 pm - Muzammil New: ʿUmar ibn al-Khaṭṭāb (may Allāh be pleased with him) used to say Takbīr in his tent in Minā during those days (of Tashrīq). The people in the Masjid would hear him and say Takbīr, and the people in the marketplaces would also hear them and say Takbīr, until Minā would resound with Takbīr.

_[Akhbār Makkah by al-Fākihī (2582), al-Sunan al-Kubrā (6338); Ḥasan Asanid]_

كان ‌عمر بن الخطاب-رضي الله عنه-‌يكبّر في ‌قبته بمنى تلك الأيام، فيسمعه أهل المسجد، فيكبّرون، فيسمعهم أهل الأسواق أيضا، فيكبرون حتى ترتجّ منى تكبيرا.

07/06/2025, 7:20 am - Muzammil New: 'Eid is not a concession to do Ḥarām 
______________________________

Wakī' said: we went out with Sufyān al-Thawrī on the day of 'Eid and he said: *“'Indeed the first thing we will begin our day with is lowering the gaze.”*

_[al-Wara' by ibn Abī al-Dunyā (66); Ḥasan Isnād]_

وَكِيعٌ قَالَ خَرَجْنَا مَعَ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ فِي يَوْمِ عِيدٍ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ أَوَّلَ مَا نَبْدَأُ بِهِ فِي يَوْمِنَا ‌غَضُّ ‌أَبْصَارِنَا

_[الورع لابن أبي الدنيا (٦٦) وسنده جيد]_
08/06/2025, 9:37 am - Muzammil New: Some rulings of sacrifice 
______________________________

The Messenger of Allāh ﷺ passed by a man who had placed his foot on the side of a sheep while he was sharpening his blade, and it (the sheep) was looking at him with its eyes. So he (ﷺ) said: "Could you not have done this before? Do you intend to make it die twice?"

_[Al-Ṭabarānī in al-Kabīr (11916) and al-Awsat (3590), al-Ḥākim (7802 & 7795), al-Bayhaqī in al-Kabīr (19170), and al-Mukhtārah (12/154); with Jayyid asānīd]_

مر رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم على رجل واضع رجله على صفحة شاة وهو يحد شفرته، وهي تلحظ إليه ببصرها، فقال: أفلا قبل هذا، أتريد أن تميتها موتتان 

_[الطبراني في الكبير (١١٩١٦) والأوسط (٣٥٩٠) والحاكم (٧٨٠٢ و٧٧٩٥) والبيهقي في الكبير (١٩١٧٠) والمختارة (١٢/١٥٤) بأسانيد جياد]_


Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said: "If a Muslim slaughters and forgets to mention the name of Allāh, let him eat, for indeed the Muslim has in him a name from the names of Allāh (his state of being a Muslim is an affirmation of Allāh)."

_[Al-Maʿrifah wa al-Tārīkh (2/10) and al-Ṣaghīr (4/43) by al-Bayhaqī; with Jayyid asānīd]_

عن ابن عباس قال: ‌إذا ‌ذبح ‌المسلم، ‌ونسي ‌أن ‌يذكر اسم الله فليأكل فإن المسلم فيه اسم من أسماء الله

_[المعرفة والتاريخ (٢/١٠) والكبير (١٨٨٩٢) والصغير (٤/٤٣) للبيهقي بأسانيد جياد]_

ʿAlī (may Allāh be pleased with him) said: The Messenger of Allāh ﷺ forbade (sacrificing) an animal with a broken/cut horn (ʿaḍbāʾ al-qarn) or a cut ear (ʿaḍbāʾ al-udhun).

Qatādah said: So I said to Saʿīd ibn al-Musayyib (senior Tabi’i): "What is ʿaḍbāʾ al-udhun?" He said: "If half (of the ear) or more than that is cut off."

_[Al-Ṭayālisī (99), Aḥmad (1157), al-Nasāʾī (4377), Ibn Khuzaymah (2913), al-Ṭaḥāwī in Sharḥ Maʿānī al-Āthār (5785), al-Ḥākim (1733), al-Bayhaqī in al-Kabīr (19134), and al-Mukhtārah (408); with Ḥasan asānīd]_

قال علي: نهى رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم عن ‌عضباء ‌القرن والأذن.
قال قتادة فقلت ‌لسعيد ‌بن ‌المسيب: ما ‌عضباء الأذن؟ قال: إذا كان النصف فأكثر من ذلك مقطوعًا

_[الطيالسي (٩٩) وأحمد (١١٥٧) والنسائي (٤٣٧٧) وابن خزيمة (٢٩١٣) والطحاوي في شرح معاني الآثار (٥٧٨٥) والحاكم (١٧٣٣) والبيهقي في الكبير (١٩١٣٤) والمختارة (٤٠٨) بأسانيد حسان]_

Ḥujayyah ibn ʿAdī said: I heard a man asking ʿAlī (may Allāh be pleased with him), saying: "I bought this cow for sacrifice?" He (ʿAlī) said: "(It can be) on behalf of seven (people)." The man asked: "The horn (if broken/damaged)?" He (ʿAlī) said: "It does not harm you." The man asked: "And a limp?" He (ʿAlī) said: "(It is okay) as long as it can walk to the place of sacrifice." Then he (ʿAlī) said: "Allāh’s Messenger ﷺ commanded us to thoroughly inspect the eye and the ear."

_[Aḥmad (826 & 1021), al-Dārimī (1972), and al-Ḥākim (7767); with Ḥasan asānīd]_ (1)

عن حجية بن عدي قال: سمعت رجلا سأل عليا قال: إني اشتريت هذه ‌البقرة للأضحى؟ قال: عن ‌سبعة. قال: القرن؟ قال: ‌لا ‌يضرك. قال: العرج؟ قال: إذا بلغت المنسك. ثم قال: أمرنا رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم أن نستشرف العين والأذن 

_[أحمد (٨٢٦ و١٠٢١) والدارمي (١٩٧٢) والحاكم (٧٧٦٧) بأسانيد حسان]_

_______________________________
(1) This shows small defects are forgiven

11/06/2025, 9:11 am - +91 63887 26284: Assalamu alaikum Warahmatullah wabarakatuh

ʿAlī ibn Abī Ṭālib رضي الله عنه said :

وقال ﷺ : يُوشك أن لا يبقى من الإسلام إلا اسمه، ومن القرآن إلا رسمه، مساجدهم يومئذ عامرة وهي خراب من الهدى، علماؤهم شرّ من تحت أديم السماء، من عندهم تخرج الفتنة، وفيهم تعود

There will come a time when nothing will remain of Islām except its name, and nothing will remain of the Qurʾān except its script. 

The people’s mosques will be full, but empty of guidance. Their scholars will be the worst of people under the sky; from them, fitnah will emerge, and to them it will return.

ابطال الحيل (18)

“Whoever settles in the land of the non-Arabs and celebrates their new year and festival and imitates them until he dies while he is in that state, will be gathered with them on the Day of Resurrection.”

11/06/2025, 11:46 am - Mohamed Ahmed Abdulwahab: Sahih Muslim 360

Jabir b. Samura reported:
A man asked the Messenger of Allah (may peace he upon him) whether he should perform ablution after (eating) mutton. He (the Messenger of Allah) said: Perform ablution it you so desire, and if you do not wish, do not perform it. *He (again) asked: Should I perform ablution (after eating) camel's flesh? He said: Yes, perform ablution (after eating) camel's flesh*

17/06/2025, 3:52 pm - Mohamed Ahmed Abdulwahab: The Ṣaḥābah didn't just recite the Qurān 
______________________________

Abū ʿAbd al-Raḥmān al-Sulamī (Tābi'ī) said:
*"Indeed, we took the Qurʾān from a people who informed us that they, when they learned ten Āyāt, would not proceed to the next ten until they acted upon the knowledge contained within them. He said: So we learned knowledge and action together. And indeed, this Qurʾān will be inherited by a people after us who will drink it as they drink water (recite it quickly), it will not go beyond their collarbones. He said: Nay, it will not go beyond here – and he placed his hand under his chin."*

_[Al-Bidaʿ wa al-Nahy ʿanhā (255), Faḍāʾil al-Qurʾān by al-Firyābī (169), and al-Ṭabaqāt (8/292); with Jayyid asānīd]_

عَنْ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ ‌السُّلَمِيِّ قَالَ: " إِنَّا أَخَذْنَا الْقُرْآنَ عَنْ قَوْمٍ ، فَأَخْبَرُونَا أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا إِذَا تَعَلَّمُوا ‌عَشْرَ آيَاتٍ لَمْ يُجَاوِزُوهُنَّ إِلَى ‌الْعَشْرِ الْأُخَرِ حَتَّى يَعْمَلُوا مَا فِيهِنَّ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ ، قَالَ: فَتَعَلَّمْنَا الْعِلْمَ وَالْعَمَلَ جَمِيعًا ، وَإِنَّهُ سَيَرِثُ هَذَا الْقُرْآنَ قَوْمٌ بَعْدَنَا يَشْرَبُونَهُ كَشُرْبِهِمُ الْمَاءَ ، لَا يُجَاوِزُ تَرَاقِيَهُمْ ، قَالَ: بَلْ لَا يُجَاوِزُ هَهُنَا ، وَوَضَعَ يَدَهُ تَحْتَ حَنَكِهِ "

[البدع والنهي عنها (٢٥٥) وفضائل القرآن للفريابي (١٦٩) والطبقات (٨/٢٩٢) بأسانيد جيدة]
17/06/2025, 8:07 pm - Abdullah PFP design Mustafa: السَّــــــــــــلَامْ عَلَيْـــــــــــــــــكم وَرَحْمَةُ اللهِ وَبَرْكَاتُهُ

Imam ash-Shafi’ee (may Allah have mercy upon him) said:

لَيْسَ مِنْ قَوْمٍ لا يُخْرِجُونَ نِسَاءَهُمْ إِلَى رِجَالِ غَيْرِهِمْ فِي التَّزْوِيجِ ، وَلا رِجَالَهُمْ إِلَى نِسَاءِ غَيْرِهِمْ فِي التَّزْوِيجِ ، إِلا جَاءَ أَوْلادُهُمْ حَمْقَى

“There is not a group of people who do not bring forth their women to marry men other than their own men, nor do their men go forth to marry women other than their own, except their children will be fools (i.e. born with a mental defect)” [Adaab ash-Shaafi’ee wa Manaaqibuhu (pg. 99) with a Saheeh chain of narration]

Ibn Abi Mulaykah reported: Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, said to the house of Al-Sa’ib, “You have become frail, so marry intelligent people unrelated to you.”

Al-Shafi’i said, “Whenever the people of a household do not allow their women to marry men outside of their line, there will be fools among their children.”

Source: al-Talkhīṣ al-Ḥabīr 1371

عَنْ ابْنِ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ قَالَ قَالَ عُمَرُ بن الخطاب رضي الله عنه لِآلِ السَّائِبِ قَدْ أَضْوَأْتُمْ فَانْكِحُوا فِي النَّوَابِغِ يَعْنِي تَزَوَّجُوا الْغَرَائِبَ

قَالَ الشَّافِعِي أَيُّمَا أَهْلِ بَيْتٍ لَمْ تَخْرُجْ نِسَاؤُهُمْ إلَى رِجَالٍ غَيْرِهِمْ كَانَ فِي أَوْلَادِهِمْ حُمْقٌ

______________________________

ʿAbdullāh bin ʿUmar (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said:
*"Sitting between the shade and the sun is the sitting place of Shayṭān."*

_[Muṣannaf Ibn Abī Shaybah (27635); Isnād Ṣaḥīḥ]_

عبد اللَّه ابن عمر يقول: القعود ‌بين ‌الظل ‌والشمس مقعد ‌الشيطان

21/06/2025, 9:52 am - Muzammil New: https://salafiri.com/knowledge_worship
22/06/2025, 3:16 pm - Muzammil New: Etiquettes of drinking Zamzam
_______________________________

Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said that he indeed saw a man drinking from the water of Zamzam, so he said: "Do you know how to drink from the water of Zamzam?" The man said: "And how should I drink from the water of Zamzam, O Abā ʿAbbās?" He (Ibn ʿAbbās) said: "When you intend to drink from the water of Zamzam, draw a bucketful from it, then face the Qiblah, and say: Bismillāh and drink in three breaths until you are filled. Then say: 'Allāhumma innī asʾaluka ʿilman nāfiʿā, wa rizqan wāsiʿan, wa shifāʾan min kulli dāʾ.' (O Allāh, indeed, I ask You for beneficial knowledge, and abundant provision, and a cure from every disease)."

_[Akhbār Makkah by al-Fākihī (1107); Isnād Ḥasan]_

عن ابن عباس رضي الله عنهما قال: إنّه رأى رجلا يشرب من ماء زمزم، فقال: هل تدري كيف تشرب من ماء زمزم؟ قال: وكيف أشرب من ماء زمزم يا أبا عباس؟ فقال: إذا أردت أن تشرب من ماء زمزم فانزع دلوا منها ثم استقبل القبلة، وقل: بسم الله، وتنفّس ثلاثا حتى تضلّع، وقل: الّلهم إنّي أسألك علما نافعا، ورزقا واسعا، وشفاء من كل داء.

[أخبار مكة للفاكهي (1107) وسنده حسن]
23/06/2025, 6:09 pm - Muzammil New: Permissibility of giving back loan with something extra
______________________________

ʿAṭāʾ was asked about a man who lends another man dirhams, and then he gives him (in return) better than what he took from him, without him asking for it. He (ʿAṭāʾ) said: "There is no harm in it. ʿAbd Allāh ibn ʿUmar borrowed some white dirhams from a man, then he repaid him with black dirhams in full. The man said to him: 'This is better than what I gave you!' ʿAbd Allāh ibn ʿUmar said to him: 'I know, but I have made it permissible for you.'"

_[Musaddad as in Itḥāf al-Khiyarah al-Maharah (3/378), Ibn Abī Shaybah (24252), al-Ṭabarānī (13071), ʿAbd al-Razzāq (15516), Mālik (2507), and al-Awsat by Ibn al-Mundhir (8223); with Ṣaḥīḥ asānīd]_

Imām Mālik said (2508): There is no harm for one who has taken loan of gold, silver, food, or animals to receive from the one who gave it to him something better than what he gave him, provided that this was not based on a condition, a promise, nor a customary practice. 

سئل عطاء عن الرجل يقرض الرجل الدراهم ثم يعطيه أفضل مما أخذ منه من غير أن يسأله إياه؟ قال: لا بأس به، قد استقرض عبد الله بن عمر من رجل دراهم بيضاء عددا ثم قضاه سوداء وافية، فقال له صاحبه: هذا أفضل مما أعطيتك! فقال له عبد الله بن عمر: قد علمت ولكني قد أحللته لك

[مسدد كما في إتحاف الخيرة المهرة (٣/٣٧٨) وابن أبي شيبة (٢٤٢٥٢) والطبراني (١٣٠٧١) وعبد الرزاق (١٥٥١٦) ومالك (٢٥٠٧) والأوسط لابن المنذر (٨٢٢٣) بأسانيد صحيحة]

قال مالك: لَا بَأْسَ بِأَنْ يُقْبِضَ مَنْ أُسْلِفَ شَيْئاً مِنَ الذَّهَبِ أَوِ الْوَرِقِ أَوِ الطَّعَامِ أَوِ الْحَيَوَانِ مِمَّنْ أَسْلَفَهُ ذلِكَ أَفْضَلَ مِمَّا أَسْلَفَهُ. إِذَا لَمْ يَكُنْ ذلِكَ عَلَى شَرْطٍ أَوْ وَأْيٍ أَوْ عَادَةٍ. فَإِنْ كَانَ ذلِكَ عَلَى شَرْطٍ، أَوْ وَأْيٍ أَوْ عَادَةٍ. فَذلِكَ مَكْرُوهٌ وَلَا خَيْرَ فِيهِ

23/06/2025, 6:26 pm - Muzammil New: Hence the conditions below
24/06/2025, 10:55 am - Muzammil New: Youth is from puberty to 40 years
_______________________________

Allāh ﷻ said: _{Until, when he reaches his full strength and reaches forty years, he says, "My Lord, enable me..."}_ [Al-Aḥqāf: 15]. And He said: _{And when he reached his full strength and achieved maturity...}_ [Al-Qaṣaṣ: 14]. And He said: _{Did We not grant you life long enough for whoever would remember therein to remember, and the warner came to you?}_ [Fāṭir: 37].
The Prophet ﷺ said: _“Allāh has left no excuse for a person whose life He prolonged until he reached sixty years of age.”_ [Al-Bukhārī (6419)]

Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said:
*His full strength is thirty-three years, and his maturity is forty years, and the age concerning which Allāh has left no excuse for the son of Ādam is sixty.*

_[Tafsīr al-Ṭabarī (21/139) and Tafsīr al-Thaʿlabī (2127); Isnād Ḥasan]_

عن ابن عباس، قال: أَشُدُّه: ثلاث وثلاثون سنةً، واسْتَواؤُه: أربعون سنةً، والعمرُ الذي أعذَر الله فيه إلى ابن آدمَ: ستون.

[تفسير الطبري (٢١/١٣٩) وتفسير الثعلبي (٢١٢٧) وسنده حسن]
25/06/2025, 10:50 am - Muzammil New: Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said: *"Indeed, the Kursī which encompasses the heavens and the earth is the place of the two feet (of Allāh).* (1) And none can estimate the extent of the ʿArsh (Throne) except the One Who created it. And indeed, the heavens in (relation to) the creation of al-Raḥmān, blessed and exalted is He – are like a dome in a desert."

_[Al-Sunnah by ʿAbdullāh (590 & 1091) and al-ʿAẓamah by Abī al-Shaykh (2/552); Isnād Ḥasan]_

عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ رضي الله عنهما، قَالَ: إِنَّ الْكُرْسِيَّ الَّذِي وَسِعَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ لِمَوْضِعِ الْقَدَمَيْنِ، ‌وَمَا ‌يُقَدِّرُ ‌قَدْرَ ‌الْعَرْشِ ‌إِلَّا ‌الَّذِي ‌خَلَقَهُ، ‌وَإِنَّ ‌السَّمَاوَاتِ ‌فِي ‌خَلْقِ ‌الرَّحْمَنِ تبارك وتعالى مِثْلُ قُبَّةٍ فِي صَحْرَاءَ

[السنة لعبد الله (٥٩٠ و١٠٩١) والعظمة لأبي الشيخ (٢/٥٥٢) وسنده حسن]

_______________________________
(1) Al-Azharī (d. 370 AH) said:
And this is a narration upon whose authenticity the people of knowledge have consensus upon. As for what has been narrated from Ibn ʿAbbās regarding the Kursī that it is knowledge, then it is not from what the knowledgeable ones regarding narrations approve (its authenticity).

[Tahdhīb al-Lughah 10/33]

قال الأزهري (ت ٣٧٠):
وَهَذِه روايةٌ اتفقَ أَهْلُ ‌العلمِ على صِحتها، وَالَّذِي رُوِيَ عَن ‌ابْن ‌عَبَّاس فِي ‌الكُرْسيّ أنَّهُ ‌العِلمُ، فَليسَ ممّا يُثبتُه أَهلُ المعرِفةِ بالأخبارِ.

[تهذيب اللغة ١٠/٣٣]

28/06/2025, 1:39 pm - Muzammil New: The Prophet ﷺ said: *"There will not cease to be a group of my Ummah fighting upon the truth, victorious until the Day of Resurrection."*

*(Al-Imām) al-Bukhārī said: Meaning*
*the Ahl al-Ḥadīth.*

_[Al-Ḥujjah fī Bayān al-Maḥajjah (1/262); Isnād Ḥasan]_


النَّبِي ﷺ يَقُولُ "لَا تَزَالُ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ أُمَّتِي يُقَاتِلُونَ عَلَى الْحَقِّ ظَاهِرِينَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ"

________________________________

ʿĀʾishah (may Allāh be pleased with her), that she was mentioned in the presence of a man, and he insulted her. So it was said to him: "Is she not your mother?" He said: "She is not a mother to me." _[Al-Ḥujjah fī Bayān al-Maḥajjah (2/402); Isnād Ḥasan]_

عَنْ عَائِشَةَ رضي الله عنها أَنَّهَا ذُكِرَتْ عِنْدَ رَجُلٍ فَسَبَّهَا. فَقِيلَ لَهُ: أَلَيْسَتْ أُمَّكَ؟ قَالَ: مَا هِيَ بِأُمٍّ فَبَلَغَهَا ذَلِكَ فَقَالَتْ: صَدَقَ إِنَّمَا ‌أَنَا ‌أُمُّ ‌الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَأَمَّا الْكَافِرِينَ فَلَسْتُ لَهُمْ بِأُمٍّ.

02/07/2025, 9:47 am - +92 300 8233395: *YOU WILL GET ADDICTED TO ISTIGHFAR AFTER READING THIS*

The Beautiful story of Imam Ahmad Ibn Hanbal and the Baker from Tafseer Al-Qurtubi رحمه الله (18/301-302

During his old age, Imam Ahmad, a renowned scholar of Islam and a famous theologian, was traveling when he stopped by a town. After salah (prayer), he wanted to stay for the night in the mosque. Owing to his humility, he hadn't introduced himself to anyone thinking that if he did, he would be welcomed by many people.

Failing to recognize Ahmad bin Hanbal, the caretaker of the mosque refused to let him stay in the mosque. A baker, whose shop was nearby, watched this scene and took pity on Imam Ahmed. He invited the Imam to stay with him for the night.

He watched as the baker mixed and kneaded the dough, tended the fire, and pulled hot loaves from the oven, all the while uttering remembrances of Allah and Istighfar

In the morning, the Imam eagerly asked his host about the latter's continual istighfaar. The baker said it had become like second nature, and Imam Ahmad then asked whether the man had experienced any reward from this practice.

The baker answered, "By Allah! No dua I made except that it was answered but one." When Ibn Hanbal asked what that unanswered prayer was, the baker responded: "To see the famous Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal."

At this, tears came to Ibn Hanbal's eyes and he told the baker, "I am Ahmed ibn Hanbal!" "By Allah! I was brought to your place so that you can have your dua/wish come true."

02/07/2025, 11:58 am - +91 84930 49133: Al-Miqdam ibn Ma'dikarib and a man of Banu Asad from the people of Qinnisrin went to Mu'awiyah ibn AbuSufyan.
Mu'awiyah said to al-Miqdam: Do you know that al-Hasan ibn Ali has died? Al-Miqdam recited the Qur'anic verse "We belong to Allah and to Him we shall return."

A man asked him: Do you think it a calamity? He replied: Why should I not consider it a calamity when it is a fact that the Messenger of Allah (ﷺ) used to take him on his lap, saying: This belongs to me and Husayn belongs to Ali?

The man of Banu Asad said: (He was) a live coal which Allah has extinguished. Al-Miqdam said: Today I shall continue to make you angry and make you hear what you dislike. He then said: Mu'awiyah, if I speak the truth, declare me true, and if I tell a lie, declare me false.

He said: Do so. He said: I adjure you by Allah, did you hear the Messenger of Allah (ﷺ) forbidding use to wear gold?

He replied: Yes. He said: I adjure you by Allah, do you know that the Messenger of Allah (ﷺ) prohibited the wearing of silk?

He replied: Yes. He said: I adjure you by Allah, do you know that the Messenger of Allah (ﷺ) prohibited the wearing of the skins of beasts of prey and riding on them?

He said: Yes. He said: I swear by Allah, I saw all this in your house, O Mu'awiyah.

Mu'awiyah said: I know that I cannot be saved from you, O Miqdam.

Khalid said: Mu'awiyah then ordered to give him what he did not order to give to his two companions, and gave a stipend of two hundred (dirhams) to his son. Al-Miqdam then divided it among his companions, and the man of Banu Asad did not give anything to anyone from the property he received. When Mu'awiyah was informed about it, he said: Al-Miqdam is a generous man; he has an open hand (for generosity). The man of Banu Asad withholds his things in a good manner.

الثبوت في حق المؤلف يكون بإسناد صحيح أو بكتاب ثابت عنه

Rule would be:
ما ثبت نقله عن المؤلف في كتاب صحت نسبته إليه، فهو حجة عليه ويعد من قوله
Whatever is reported from an author in his own confirmed book is treated as his saying and is a proof.
المكتوب كالملفوظ
What is written is like what is spoken.

02/07/2025, 2:42 pm - +92 316 4986376: _"His Kursī extends over the heavens and the earth"_ [2:255]
_________________________________

Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said: *"Indeed, the Kursī which encompasses the heavens and the earth is the place of the two feet (of Allāh).* (1) And none can estimate the extent of the ʿArsh (Throne) except the One Who created it. And indeed, the heavens in (relation to) the creation of al-Raḥmān, blessed and exalted is He – are like a dome in a desert."

_[Al-Sunnah by ʿAbdullāh (590 & 1091) and al-ʿAẓamah by Abī al-Shaykh (2/552); Isnād Ḥasan]_

عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ رضي الله عنهما، قَالَ: إِنَّ الْكُرْسِيَّ الَّذِي وَسِعَ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ لِمَوْضِعِ الْقَدَمَيْنِ، ‌وَمَا ‌يُقَدِّرُ ‌قَدْرَ ‌الْعَرْشِ ‌إِلَّا ‌الَّذِي ‌خَلَقَهُ، ‌وَإِنَّ ‌السَّمَاوَاتِ ‌فِي ‌خَلْقِ ‌الرَّحْمَنِ تبارك وتعالى مِثْلُ قُبَّةٍ فِي صَحْرَاءَ

[السنة لعبد الله (٥٩٠ و١٠٩١) والعظمة لأبي الشيخ (٢/٥٥٢) وسنده حسن]

_______________________________
(1) Al-Azharī (d. 370 AH) said:
And this is a narration upon whose authenticity the people of knowledge have consensus upon. As for what has been narrated from Ibn ʿAbbās regarding the Kursī that it is knowledge, then it is not from what the knowledgeable ones regarding narrations approve (its authenticity).

[Tahdhīb al-Lughah 10/33]

قال الأزهري (ت ٣٧٠):
وَهَذِه روايةٌ اتفقَ أَهْلُ ‌العلمِ على صِحتها، وَالَّذِي رُوِيَ عَن ‌ابْن ‌عَبَّاس فِي ‌الكُرْسيّ أنَّهُ ‌العِلمُ، فَليسَ ممّا يُثبتُه أَهلُ المعرِفةِ بالأخبارِ.

Riwāyah & Dirāyah | Readings with Ijāzāt (English Explanations)

A dedicated Telegram group for attending majālis al-samā‘ — recitations of classical texts with clear English explanation (dirāyah) and opportunities for ijāzāt through authentic isnāds.

– Books of ʿAqīdah, including works of Shaykh Muḥammad ibn ʿAbd al-Wahhāb

– Explanations of ḥadīth collections and foundational texts
– Shorter mutoon across various Islamic sciences (ʿaqīdah, fiqh, uṣūl, adab)

*The Punishment Of An Innovator!*

Muhammad b. Ismā'il at-Taymī رحمه الله said: "I read in some narrations that, upon hearing the words of the Prophet ﷺ: "*If one of you awaken from sleep, then he should not dip his hand in a container unless washes his hand because he does not know where it was while he was sleeping,*"

An innovator said: "I know where my hands went while in bed, so I do not have to fulfil this command!"

Consequently, upon waking up the next morning, his hand - up to the forearm - was found inserted in his anus."

📚 [بستان العارفين للإمام النووي ٥٠]
04/07/2025, 10:52 am - محمد عبد الوهاب: السلام عليكم ورحمة الله وبركاته 

Al-Baihaqi also reported on the authority of `Aamir ibn Sa`d , that his father said: 

 A Bedouin came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺand said: ―My father used to uphold ties of kinship, and he did such-and-such (mentioning his acts of kindness), so where is he? The Prophet ﷺ said: He is in the Fire. The Bedouin found it difficult to bear.  Then he said: ―Where is your father oh Messenger of Allah? He ﷺsaid: Whenever you pass by the grave of an idolater, give him the tidings of Hell-fire.  The Bedouin later became Muslim, and he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ gave me a difficult task. I never passed the grave of an idolater, but I gave him the tidings of Hellfire.

Al-Baihaqi in Ad-Dalail‘ (1/191-192), and also reported by At Ṭabarani in Al-Kabeer (326), as well as by Ad-Dhiyaa‘ Al-Maqdasee in Al-Mukhtaarah‘ (1005) 

Authenticity please

04/07/2025, 2:55 pm - +91 92842 66378: Perfection In A Wife?

Shaykh Muhammad Ibn Al-Uthaymeen [D.1421 A.H.] [رحمه الله] said:

❝Indeed many husbands want their wives to be perfect. This matter is not possible, so due to that husbands fall into worry and concern and are incapable of enjoyment and delight with their wives, and perhaps this could lead to divorce.

Just like the Messenger [ﷺ] said:

«وإن ذهبت تقيمها كسرتها وكسرها طلاقها.»

'If you tried to straighten her you would break her, and breaking her is divorcing her.'

Therefore, it is necessary for the husband to be easy going and overlook everything that a wife does as long as it does not contradict the Deen or nobility.❞

[Haqooq Da'at Ilayhi Al Fitra, (No. 22)]

Al-Ṭabarī said concerning the views from the Ṣaḥābah/Salaf on this Ḥadīth : 

• When one feels safe and protected from harm. This was narrated from Ibn Masʿūd and Ḥudhayfah, and was the view of Usāmah رضي الله عنهم. 

• Others (from the Ṣaḥābah) said : Whoever sees wrongdoing from a ruler must denounce it publicly, if possible — narrated from ʿUmar and Ubayy ibn Kaʿb رضي الله عنهما.

• Others said : One must denounce it inwardly (in his heart).

كتاب عمدة القاري شرح صحيح البخاري (15/166)

06/07/2025, 12:59 pm - Muzammil New: *Some narrations regarding ʿĀshūrāʾ*

*ʿAbd al-Raḥmān ibn ʿAwf had his morning meal on the Day of ʿĀshūrāʾ until the day had well risen (forenoon) while he was unaware. Then he came to know afterwards and became alarmed by that. He then fasted and commanded us to do the Ṣiyām, after he (already) had his morning meal.* (1)

[Tahdhīb al-Āthār - Musnad ʿUmar (657); Isnād Ṣaḥīḥ]

عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ عَوْفٍ أَنَّهُ أَضْحَى يَوْمَ عَاشُورَاءَ حَتَّى ارْتَفَعَ النَّهَارُ وَلَا يَعْلَمُ، ثُمَّ عَلِمَ بَعْدُ، فَفَزِعَ لِذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ صَامَ، وَأَمَرَنَا بِالصِّيَامِ بَعْدَ أَنْ أَضْحَى

[تهذيب الآثار - مسند عمر (٦٥٧) وسنده صحيح] 

Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) says regarding the Day of ʿĀshūrāʾ:
*"Differ from the Jews, and fast the ninth and the tenth."*

[Muṣannaf ʿAbd al-Razzāq (8086), Sharḥ Maʿānī al-Āthār (3085), al-Sunan al-Kabīr (8478), Shuʿab al-Īmān (3509), and Faḍāʾil al-Awqāt (242); with Jayyid asānīd]

ابن ‌عباس يقول في يوم عاشوراء: خالفوا ‌اليهود، وصوموا ‌التاسع والعاشر.

[مصنف عبد الرزاق (٨٠٨٦) وشرح معاني الآثار (٣٠٨٥) والسنن الكبير (٨٤٧٨) وشعب الإيمان (٣٥٠٩) وفضائل الأوقات (٢٤٢) بأسانيد جياد] 

Ibn ʿAbbās (may Allāh be pleased with them both) *used to fast a day before it and a day after it.* (2)

[Tahdhīb al-Āthār - Musnad ʿUmar (660); Isnād Ṣaḥīḥ]

عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَصُومُ قَبْلَهُ يَوْمًا وَبَعْدَهُ يَوْمًا

[تهذيب الآثار - مسند عمر (٦٦٠) وسنده صحيح] 

*Ṭāwūs used to fast a day before it and a day after it out of fear that he would miss it.*

[Muṣannaf Ibn Abī Shaybah (9630); Isnād Ṣaḥīḥ]

عن ابن طاوس عن أبيه أنه كان يصوم قبله وبعده يومًا مخافة أن يفوته

[مصنف ابن أبي شيبة (٩٦٣٠) وسنده صحيح] 

al-Rubayyiʿ bint Muʿawwidh, may Allah be pleased with her said:
*"...and we would make our young children fast, if Allāh willed. We would go to the Masjid and make for them a toy from carded wool. If one of them cried for food, we would give it to him (to play with) at the time of Iftār."*

[Muslim (1136)]

وَنُصَوِّمُ صِبْيَانَنَا الصِّغَارَ مِنْهُمْ إِنْ شَاءَ اللهُ، وَنَذْهَبُ إِلَى الْمَسْجِدِ فَنَجْعَلُ لَهُمُ اللُّعْبَةَ مِنَ الْعِهْنِ، فَإِذَا بَكَى أَحَدُهُمْ عَلَى الطَّعَامِ أَعْطَيْنَاهَا إِيَّاهُ عِنْدَ الْإِفْطَارِ [مسلم (١١٣٦)]

------------------------------
(1) Also see al-Bukhari 2007
(2) Note: the Marfu' narrations are weak

Ibn al-Qayyim (D. 751) said:
"Nothing of it (regarding ʿĀshūrāʾ) is authentic, not even a single ḥadīth. And nothing is established from the Prophet ﷺ regarding it other than the aḥādīth about fasting it. And whatever besides that is baseless."

[Al-Manār al-Munīf (p. 103)]

07/07/2025, 4:47 pm - محمد مبشر: ~Free your Heart 

Anas ibn Malik reported: The Messenger of Allaah, peace and blessings be upon him, said to me: 

يَا بُنَيَّ إِنْ قَدَرْتَ أَنْ تُصْبِحَ وَتُمْسِيَ لَيْسَ فِي قَلْبِكَ غِشٌّ لِأَحَدٍ فَافْعَلْ
Young man, if you are able every morning and evening to remove any malevolence in your heart towards anyone, then do so.

Then, the Prophet said to me:
يَا بُنَيَّ وَذَلِكَ مِنْ سُنَّتِي وَمَنْ أَحْيَا سُنَّتِي فَقَدْ أَحَبَّنِي وَمَنْ أَحَبَّنِي كَانَ مَعِي فِي الْجَنَّة
Young man, that is my Sunnah. Whoever revives my Sunnah has loved me, and whoever loves me will be with me in Paradise.
 Sunan al-Tirmidhi‌ 2678, Grade: Hasan

Yaḥyá bin Sa'īd al-Qaṭṭān (may Allah have mercy on him) said:
*Do not look at the (text of) Ḥadīth but look at the Isnād. If it is authentic (then good) otherwise do not be deceived by the Ḥadīth when the Isnād is not authentic*

_[Al-Jāmi' li Akhlāq al-Rāwī 1301; Ṣaḥīḥ Isnād]_

قال يحيى بن سعيد: لا تنظروا إلى الحديث ولكن انظروا إلى الإسناد فإن صح الإسناد وإلا فلا تغتر بالحديث إذا لم يصح الإسناد

_[الجامع لأخلاق الراوي وآداب السامع (١٣٠١) وسنده صحيح]_

09/07/2025, 9:55 pm - Muzammil New: Virtues of 'Uthmān
_______________________________

ʿAbdullāh ibn ʿUmar (may Allāh be pleased with them both) said:
*A man from the Anṣār came to me during the caliphate of ʿUthmān and spoke to me, and in his speech, he was directing me to find fault with ʿUthmān. He spoke for a long time, and he was a man with heaviness in his tongue, so he could hardly finish his words smoothly. He (Ibn ʿUmar) said: When he finished his speech, I said to him: “Indeed, we used to say while the Messenger of Allāh ﷺ was alive: ‘The best of the Ummah of the Messenger of Allāh after him is Abū Bakr, then ʿUmar, then ʿUthmān.’ And indeed, by Allāh, we do not know that ʿUthmān killed any soul without right, nor did he commit any of the major sins. But it is this matter of wealth; if he gives it to you, you are pleased, and if he gives it to his relatives, you are angered. You only want to be like the Persians and the Romans, who do not leave a ruler for themselves except that they kill him.”*

[Faḍāʾil al-Ṣaḥābah by Imām Aḥmad (64) with a Ṣaḥīḥ isnād; al-Sunnah by al-Khallāl (546), al-Sharīʿah (1453), and Tārīkh Dimashq (39/159)]

عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ عُمَرَ رضي الله عنه قَالَ:
جَاءَنِي رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ فِي خِلَافَةِ عُثْمَانَ فَكَلَّمَنِي، فَإِذَا هُوَ يَأْمُرُنِي فِي كَلَامِهِ بِأَنْ أَعْيَبَ عَلَى عُثْمَانَ، فَتَكَلَّمَ كَلَامًا طَوِيلًا، وَهُوَ امْرُؤ فِي لِسَانِهِ ثِقَلٌ، فَلَمْ يَكَدْ يَقْضِي كَلَامَهُ فِي سَرِيحٍ، قَالَ: فَلَمَّا قَضَى كَلَامَهُ قُلْتُ لَهُ: إِنَّا كُنَّا نَقُولُ وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم حَيٌّ: أَفْضَلُ أُمَّةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ بَعْدَهُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، ثُمَّ عُمَرُ، ثُمَّ عُثْمَانُ، وَإِنَّا وَاللَّهِ مَا نَعْلَمُ عُثْمَانَ قَتَلَ نَفْسًا بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ، وَلَا جَاءَ مِنَ الْكَبَائِرِ شَيْئًا، وَلَكِنْ هُوَ هَذَا الْمَالُ، فَإِنْ أَعْطَاكُمُوهُ رَضِيتُمْ، وَإِنْ أَعْطَاهُ أُولِي قَرَابَتِهِ سَخِطْتُمْ، إِنَّمَا تُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَكُونُوا كَفَارِسَ وَالرُّومِ، لَا يَتْرُكُونَ لَهُمْ أَمِيرًا إِلَّا قَتَلُوهُ 

[فضائل الصحابة للإمام أحمد (٦٤) بإسناد صحيح والسنة للخلال (٥٤٦) والشريعة (١٤٥٣) وتاريخ دمشق (١٥٩/٣٩)]

With a different wording, it's narrated from Anas bin Malik in Sahih al Bukhari

Chapter: No time will come but the time following it will be worse than it
باب لاَ يَأْتِي زَمَانٌ إِلاَّ الَّذِي بَعْدَهُ شَرٌّ مِنْهُ

Narrated Az-Zubair bin `Adi:
We went to Anas bin Malik and complained about the wrong we were suffering at the hand of Al- Hajjaj. Anas bin Malik said, "Be patient till you meet your Lord, for no time will come upon you but the time following it will be worse than it. I heard that from the Prophet."

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يُوسُفَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ الزُّبَيْرِ بْنِ عَدِيٍّ، قَالَ أَتَيْنَا أَنَسَ بْنَ مَالِكٍ فَشَكَوْنَا إِلَيْهِ مَا نَلْقَى مِنَ الْحَجَّاجِ فَقَالَ ‏ "‏ اصْبِرُوا، فَإِنَّهُ لاَ يَأْتِي عَلَيْكُمْ زَمَانٌ إِلاَّ الَّذِي بَعْدَهُ شَرٌّ مِنْهُ، حَتَّى تَلْقَوْا رَبَّكُمْ ‏"‏‏.‏ سَمِعْتُهُ مِنْ نَبِيِّكُمْ صلى الله عليه وسلم‏.‏
Sahih al-Bukhari 7068
https://sunnah.com/bukhari:7068

• Three Things sickens the body:

1) talking too much.
2) sleeping too much
3) eating too much.

• Four things destroys the body:

1) stress.
2) grief.
3) staying up late at night.
4) hunger

• Four things brings Rizq (provision):

1) Night full prayers
2) frequent remembrance of Allah before
dawn.
3) continuous charity
4) the remembrance of Allah at the beginning and at the end of the day.

• Four things prevents Rizq (provision):

1) Sleeping early in the morning (after Fajr). 2) lack of prayers.
3) laziness.
4) treason and betrayal.

• Four things dries the face and takes away its joy and respect:

1) lying.
2) insolence.
3) asking too many questions without
knowledge.
4) indecency.

• Four things brings to the face joy and respect:

1) piety.
2) truthfulness
3) generosity
4) self respect.

Mashallah, my dear brothers 🌹

I am pleased to introduce to you a new member with us in this council, our diligent Hafiz, holder of high chains of narration, and a shining student of hadith, Hafiz Usman Farooqi from Abbottabad. May Allah protect him and bless him.

He is in his eighth year at the College of Hadith at the University of Abi Bakr Al-Islamiya. He studied knowledge under great scholars, including our Shaykh Abdullah Nasir Rahmani, Shaykh Ghulam Mustafa Ambori, and other honorable scholars.

I recently had the honor of meeting him when we were granted the chance to visit the university. He was an excellent guide and companion. May Allah reward him well on our behalf.

I ask Allah to guide his steps in seeking hadith, to make him a blessing wherever he is, and to benefit the schools and scholarly journals he writes for and works with.

We hope he will be a strong and supportive presence here in this field. So welcome, our brother Hafiz Usman, @⁨~Hafiz Usman Farooqi⁩ . May Allah increase your success and guidance. 🌷

(١) عالم کی لغزش دین کو اس لیے گرا دیتی ہے کہ لوگ اُس کی پیروی کرتے ہیں۔ یوں اُس کی زلّت پھیل جاتی ہے، حتیٰ کہ گویا وہ سنّت (جس کی پیروی کی جائے) بن جاتی ہے۔

(٢) منافق آیاتِ قرآنیہ سے استدلال کر کے لوگوں کو بہکاتا ہے، حق کو باطل میں گڈمڈ کر دیتا ہے، اور گمراہی کا جال بچھاتا ہے۔

(٣) ایسے پیشوا / امام جو خود راہِ راست سے بھٹک جائیں، قوم کو بھی ضلالت کی راہوں پر ڈال دیتے ہیں۔ جب وہ بگڑ جاتے ہیں، پوری امت بگڑ جاتی ہے۔ رسول اللہ ﷺ نے فرمایا:
"امام ڈھال ہے۔" (مسلم ۱۸۴۱)
تو سوچیے، اگر وہی راہِ خطا پر چل پڑے تو کیا ہوگا؟

14/07/2025, 2:17 pm - Muzammil New: Virtue of saying Alḥamdulillāhi kathīran 
______________________________

Salmān (al-Fārisī, may Allah be pleased with him) said:
*A person said Alḥamdulillāhi kathīran so the angel regarded it as something too great to be written down (in reward) until he returned to his Rabb and He said: "Write it as my worshipper said "kathīran" (a lot)"*

_[al-Zuhd by Aḥmad (822); Isnād Ṣaḥīḥ]_

عن سلمان قال: قال رجل الحمد لله كثيرا قال فأعظمها الملك أن يكتبها حتى راجع فيها ربه عز وجل قال: اكتبها كما قال عبدي كثيرا

_[الزهد لأحمد (٨٢٢) وسنده صحيح]_

14/07/2025, 10:06 pm - Mohamed Ahmed Abdulwahab: *Good News of a Rare Hadith* (Authenticated by @⁨Muzammil New⁩)

Abu Umāmah (may Allah be pleased with him said: The Messenger of Allāh ﷺ said:
*“Whoever goes in morning to the Masjid (al-Nabawī), desiring nothing except to learn something good or to teach it, would have the reward of one who performs ʿUmrah, a complete ʿUmrah. And whoever goes in evening to the Masjid, desiring nothing except to learn something good or to teach it, for him is the reward of a pilgrim (Ḥājj), a complete Ḥajj (pilgrimage).”*
[Al-Mustadrak by al-Ḥākim (314); Isnād Ḥasan]

عَنْ أَبِي أُمَامَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللهِ ﷺ: مَنْ غَدَا إِلَى الْمَسْجِدِ لَا يُرِيدُ إِلَّا لِيَتَعَلَّمَ خَيْرًا، أَوْ يُعَلِّمَهُ كَانَ لَهُ أَجْرُ مُعْتَمِرٍ تَامِّ الْعُمْرَةِ، وَمَنْ رَاحَ إِلَى الْمَسْجدِ لَا يُرِيدُ إِلا لِيَتَعَلَّمَ خَيْرًا، أَوْ يُعَلِّمَهُ فَلَهُ أَجْرُ حَاجٍّ تَامِّ الْحَجَّةِ
[المستدرك للحاكم (٣١٤) وسنده حسن] <This message was edited>

Shaykh al-Islām Ibn Taymiyyah رحمه الله: 

“Just as lowering the gaze includes not looking at the ‘awrahs of other people and other haraam things, it also includes refraining from looking into people’s houses. A man’s house conceals his body just as his garments conceal him. Allaah has mentioned lowering the gaze and guarding one’s private parts after the verse about asking for permission to enter, because the house covers a person just as the clothes on his body do.”

[Majmū’ al-Fatāwā, (15/379)]

16/07/2025, 12:46 pm - Muzammil New: *Whoever desires honour then to Allah belongs all honour* [35:10]
_______________________________

Ṭāriq bin Shihāb said:
*’Umar bin al-Khaṭṭāb set out for Shām while Abu 'Ubaydah ibn al-Jarrāḥ was with us. They came upon a shallow ford and 'Umar was on his camel. He dismounted from it, took off his Khuffayn (leather socks), placed them on his shoulder, and took the reins of his camel then waded with it through the ford. Abu 'Ubaydah said, O Amir al-Muminin, are you doing this? You take off your Khuffain and place them on your shoulder, and take the reins of your camel, and crossed with it through the ford? It would not please me if the people of the country were to see you in this state. ‘Umar said: Awih! (an expression of disappointment). If anyone other than you, O Abu 'Ubaydah, had said this, I would have made him (by punishment) an example for the Ummah of Muhammad  ﷺ. Indeed we were the most humiliated people and Allah gave us honour through Islam. So whenever we seek honour through other than what Allah has honoured us with, Allah will humiliate us.*

[al-Mustadrak 207,4529; Ṣaḥīḥ asānīd]

خرج عمر بن الخطاب إلى الشام، ومعنا أبو عبيدة بن الجراح، فأتوا على مخاضة، وعمر على ناقة له، فنزل عنها، وخلع خفيه، فوضعهما على عاتقه، وأخذ بزمام ناقته، فخاض بها المخاضة، فقال أبو عبيدة: يا أمير المؤمنين، أأنت تفعل هذا، أتخلع خفيك وتضعهما على عاتقك، وتأخذ بزمام ناقتك، ‌وتخوض ‌بها ‌المخاضة؟ ما يسرني أن أهل البلد استشرفوك. فقال عمر: أوه، لو يقل ذا غيرك أبا عبيدة، جعلته نكالا لأمة محمد ﷺ، إنا كنا أذل قوم فأعزنا الله بالإسلام، فمهما نطلب العزة بغير ما أعزنا الله به أذلنا الله

_[المستدرك (207) و(4529) وسندهما صحيح]_

16/07/2025, 7:43 pm - +92 316 4986376: Even if it is regarded sahih by shaykh, he considered it to be against the way of sahabah.


Shaykh Al Albani رحمه الله:
The one who narrated raising the hands when doing rukūʿ is more firmly established, while Ibn Masʿūd رضي الله عنه denied it. Despite the high status of Ibn Masʿūd, we say that a narration that affirms something is given priority over one that denies it (إن المُثْبِت مُقَدَّم على النافي)

Imam al-Bukhārī, truly the leader of the believers in ḥadīth wrote a special treatise known as رفع اليدين في الصلاة

In it, he argued against the people of Kūfa, who did not accept the ḥadīths about Rafa ul Yadayn when going into rukūʿ and rising from it. It’s not that the ḥadīths were unknown to them, no, they were right before their eyes but because of a doubt that occurred to them, they left acting upon these well-established aḥadīth.

https://shamela.ws/book/145204/1429#p5
16/07/2025, 7:55 pm - Muzammil New: الله يرضى عليك
16/07/2025, 7:56 pm - Muzammil New: Shaykh al-Albāni رحمه الله himself said something similar under this Ḥadīth in Mishkāt al-Maṣābīḥ 

You reminded me of a similar Ḥadīth which is opposite from Abu Hurairah رضي الله عنه let me send
16/07/2025, 8:11 pm - Muzammil New: Abū Hurayrah (may Allāh be pleased with him) said:
*“I will most certainly lead you in the prayer of Allāh's Messenger ﷺ. If I am able, I will neither add nor subtract.” So he said the Takbīr and made his hands apparent (raised them) then he performed rukūʿand he neither made it long nor short. Then he raised his head and made his hands apparent, then he said the Takbīr and performed sujūd.*

[Musnad al-Shāmiyyīn (868); Isnād Ḥasan]

Abu Muti' Al-Balkhi reported: "I asked Imam Abu Hanifah about a person who says, 'I do not know whether my Rabb is, above the heavens or on earth?' Abu Hanifah (رحمه الله) said: 'A person who makes such a statement becomes an apostate because Allah, the Exalted says, 'The Merciful has ascended above the 'Arsh, and the 'Arsh of Allah is above His heavens'.

I further asked Abu Hanifah, 'What if such a person admits, Allah is above His 'Arsh, but exclaims, I do not know whether His 'Arsh is above the heavens or on earth'.

Abu Hanifah responded: 'If he denies that the 'Arsh is above the heavens, he is an apostate." [Sharh at-Tahawiyyah, p. 288] If the person apostatizes by saying that he did not know where is the 'Arsh of Allah, then by right a person who denies the Loftiness of Allah altogether is definitely worse than an apostate.

ʿAbdullāh bin Wahb said: "I saw Mālik bin Anas raising his hands when he began the prayer, and when he bowed, and when he rose from bowing." Abū ʿAbdillāh said: "So I mentioned that to Muḥammad bin ʿAbdillāh bin ʿAbd al-Ḥakam who was the representative of the companions of Mālik in Egypt and the scholar of his saying and what he died upon. 18/07/2025, 4:51 pm - Muzammil New: *_And He it is Who has created the heavens and the earth in six days and His Throne was on the water, that He may try you, which of you is the best in deeds._* [11:7]
___________________________________

ʿAbdullāh bin Masʿūd (may Allah be pleased with him) said:
*Allāh created seven heavens; the span of each one is a journey of five hundred years, and between each one of them five hundred years. And above the seven heavens is the water, and Allāh, may His praise be glorified, is above the Water. Nothing of the deeds of the children of Ādam is hidden from Him. And the earths are seven; between each earth is five hundred years, and the thickness of each earth is five hundred years.*

[Al-Dārimī in al-Radd ʿalā al-Jahmiyyah (33), al-Ṭabarī in al-Tafsīr (23/78), al-Tawḥīd by Ibn Khuzaymah (138, 139 & 598), al-Ṭabarānī (8987), al-Bayhaqī in al-Asmāʾ wa al-Ṣifāt (851), and al-Dhahabī in al-ʿUluww (74); with Ḥasan asānīd]

عن عبدِ اللهِ، قال: خلقَ اللهُ سبعَ سماواتٍ غِلَظُ كلِّ واحدةٍ مسيرةُ ‌خَمْسِمائةِ ‌عامٍ، ‌وبينَ كلِّ واحدةٍ منهنَّ ‌خمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ، وفوقَ السبعِ السماواتِ الماءُ، واللهُ جلَّ ثناؤُه فوقَ الماءِ، لا يَخْفى عليه شيءٌ مِن أعمالِ بني آدمَ. والأرضُ سَبعٌ، ‌بينَ كلِّ أرضٍ ‌خَمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ، وغِلَظُ كلِّ أرضِ ‌خَمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ

[الدارمي في الرد على الجهمية (٣٣) والطبري في التفسير (٢٣/٧٨) والتوحيد لابن خزيمة (١٣٨ و١٣٩ و598) والطبراني (٨٩٨٧) والبيهقي في الأسماء والصفات (٨٥١) والذهبي في العلو (٧٤) بأسانيد حسنة]

19/07/2025, 5:13 am - +996 505 143 155: 📜 An Interesting Tale of Mu'awiyah, The Loving Husband, And His Loyal Wife: How Marwan Forcibly Took Her With Her Father's Help And Mu'awiyah’s Justice for Them.

One day, Mu'awiyah ibn Abi Sufyan (رضي الله عنه) was holding court in Damascus when a barefoot Bedouin arrived, exhausted under the scorching sun. The man pleaded for justice his wife, Sa‘da, had been taken from him by Marwan ibn al-Hakam, the governor of Medina.  

The Injustice

- The Bedouin had married his cousin, Sa‘da, and they lived happily until tragedy struck.  

- After losing his wealth, Sa‘da’s father forcibly separated them.  

- When the Bedouin sought justice from Marwan, the governor saw his beautiful wife, imprisoned and tortured the husband, demanding he divorce her under threat of death.  
- Marwan then married Sa‘da himself.  

Mu'awiyah’s Intervention

Hearing the Bedouin’s heartbreaking poetry and plea, Mu'awiyah was furious. He wrote to Marwan:  
You have transgressed the bounds of faith! A ruler must restrain his desires if he acts like a wolf, and adulterer who will protect the flock?
  
He ordered Marwan to:  

1️⃣ Divorce Sa‘da immediately  
2️⃣ Send her back with an escort  
3️⃣ Or face severe consequences , Marwan divorced her in fear.

The Choice.

When Sa‘da was brought before Mu'awiyah, he gave her a choice and wanted to check if she really loved him:

He said, either marry:

🔸 Himself (the Caliph, with power and luxury)  
🔸 Marwan (her coercive second husband)  
🔸 The Bedouin (her first love, now impoverished)  

Without hesitation, she chose her Bedouin husband, declaring:  

"Even in hunger and rags, he is dearer to me than all the wealth and power in the world!"

Muawiyah loved her response and

 - Granted them 10,000 dirhams  
- Enrolled them in the state welfare system  
- Restored her to her true love  

The Lesson.

 True love prevails, Sa‘da remained loyal despite hardship.  
Justice is divine, Mu'awiyah rectified Marwan’s oppression.  
Women’s agency, Sa‘da’s choice was respected, a testament to her wisdom.  

Mu'awiyah, impressed by her loyalty, rewarded them generously and restored their union.  

 Reflection:

This story reminds us that real love isn’t swayed by wealth or status. True justice protects the weak, and integrity matters more than power.  

📖  Source: "Akhbar al-Nisa" by Ibn al-Jawzi pages 12 to 19, I don't know the authenticity, mentioned as ibn Jawzi quoted.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيْكَ لَهُ ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ ، يُحْيِيْ وَيُمِيْتُ ، وَهُوَ حَيٌّ لَّا يَمُوْتُ ، بِيَدِهِ الْخَيْرُ ، وَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيْرٌ

Lā ilāha illā-llahu waḥdahū lā sharīka lah, lahu-l-mulku wa lahu-l-ḥamd, yuḥyī wa yumīt, wa Huwa Ḥayyu-l-lā yamūt, bi yadihi-l-khayr, wa Huwa ʿalā kulli shay’in Qadīr.

There is no god worthy of worship except Allah. He is Alone and He has no partner. To Him Alone belong all sovereignty and all praise. He gives life and He gives death. He is Ever-Living and does not die. In His Hand is all good and He is over all things All-Powerful.

عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: مَنْ قَالَ فِي السُّوقِ: لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، لَهُ المُلْكُ وَلَهُ الحَمْدُ، يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ وَهُوَ حَيٌّ لَا يَمُوتُ، بِيَدِهِ الخَيْرُ وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ، كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لَهُ أَلْفَ أَلْفِ حَسَنَةٍ، وَمَحَا عَنْهُ أَلْفَ أَلْفِ سَيِّئَةٍ، وَبَنَى لَهُ بَيْتًا فِي الجَنَّةِ. (سنن الترمذي ٣٤٢٩)

The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: “Whoever says [the above] in the marketplace, Allah shall record a million good deeds for him, wipe a million evil deeds away from him, and build a house for him in Paradise.” (Tirmidhī 3429)

21/07/2025, 9:28 pm - +91 70061 09131: ❌ "Joining Deviants to Refute Deviants — A Betrayal of the Manhaj of the Salaf"

In recent times, we witness an alarming trend: individuals and groups aligning with one misled sect to combat another. They justify it under the guise of "strategic unity" or “greater evil vs. lesser evil.” But let it be known — this is not the way of the Salaf.

🛑 Truth is not served by compromise.
You do not extinguish a fire with fire, nor do you cure poison with poison.

📜 The Usūl of the Salaf:

🔹 Imām al-Barbahārī (d. 329H) said:

> “If you see a man sitting with a person of innovation, beware of him. For he is a man of bid’ah.”
(Sharh al-Sunnah)



🔹 Imām Ayyūb as-Sakhtiyānī said:

> “Whoever sits with a person of innovation is not safe from one of three things: either he becomes a trial for others, or something of their speech falls into his heart, or he says, ‘By Allah, I don’t care what they say.’”
(Reported by al-Lālikā’ī in Sharh Usūl I’tiqād Ahl al-Sunnah)



📌 Where Is the Ghayrah for the Sunnah?

Those who side with Ashʿarīs to refute Khawārij, or sit with Ikhwānīs to expose Shīʿa, or join Takfīrīs to fight modernists, or JOIN MATURIDIES SUFIES TO FIGHT RAWAFIDH have either lost the usūl or never knew it.

This is not hikmah — it is hizbiyyah, confusion, and betrayal.

📉 You lose clarity. You lose trust. You lose the Manhaj.

The Salaf never compromised with Ahl al-Bid‘ah to “fight a greater evil.” They held fast to clarity, even if alone.

⚔️ Allegiance in creed is a matter of religion.
You cannot borrow the sword of innovation to defend the Sunnah — it will strike you next.

💡 Ahl al-Sunnah win through clarity, not coalitions.

Let us not fall into this modern pitfall. Refuting one batil with another batil will never produce Haqq — only deeper confusion and misplaced loyalty.


---

“Stick to the truth, even if you stand alone — because the truth never feels lonely"

[Jāmiʿ Bayān al-ʿIlm (1568); Isnād Jayyid]

سُئِلَ سعيدُ بن جُبير عن شيءِ، فقال: لا أعلم. ثم قال: ويل للَّذي يقولُ لما لا يعلمُ: إني أعلم
[جامع بيان العلم (١٥٦٨) وسنده جيد]

Mālik ibn Anas (may Allāh have mercy on him) departed one day from the masjid, leaning on my hand. A man named Abū al-Juwayriyah, who was accused of al-Irjāʾ, caught up to him and said: *“O Abū ʿAbdullāh, listen to something from me so I may speak to you, debate with you, and inform you of my opinion.” He (Mālik) said: “And what if you defeat me?” He said: “If I defeat you, you will follow me.” He (Mālik) said: “And what if another man comes, speaks to us, and defeats us both?” He said: “We will follow him.” Mālik said: “O servant of Allāh, Allāh the Mighty and Majestic sent Muḥammad ﷺ with one religion, yet I see you moving from one religion to another.”*

[Al-Sharīʿah (117); Isnād Ḥasan]

ʿUmar ibn ʿAbd al-ʿAzīz said: *“He who makes his religion a point of argumentation, keeps changing the most.”*

[Al-Ṭabaqāt al-Kubrā (7/362), al-Firyābī in al-Qadar (385), al-Ājurrī (116), Ibn Abī al-Dunyā in al-Ṣamt (161), al-Faqīh wa al-Mutafaqqih (1/562), and Qiwām al-Sunnah in al-Targhīb wa al-Tarhīb (980); with Ṣaḥīḥ asānīd]

انصرف مالك بن أنس يوما من المسجد، وهو متكئ على يدي فلحقه رجل يقال له: أبو الجويرية كان يتهم بالإرجاء ، فقال: يا أبا عبد الله اسمع مني شيئا أكلمك به وأحاجك وأخبرك برأيي قال: فإن غلبتني؟ قال: إن غلبتك اتبعتني قال: فإن جاء رجل آخر، فكلمنا فغلبنا؟ قال: نتبعه قال مالك رحمه الله: يا عبد الله، بعث الله عز وجل محمدا صلى الله عليه وسلم بدين واحد، وأراك تنتقل من دين إلى دين قال عمر بن عبد العزيز: من جعل دينه غرضا للخصومات ‌أكثر ‌التنقل
[الشريعة (١١٧) وسنده حسن]

عمر بن عبد العزيز قال: من جعل دينه غرضا للخصومات ‌أكثر ‌التنقل

[الطبقات الكبرى (٧/٣٦٢) والفريابي في القدر (٣٨٥) والآجري (١١٦) وابن أبي الدنيا في الصمت (١٦١) والفقيه والمتفقه (١/٥٦٢) وقِوام السنة في الترغيب والترهيب (٩٨٠) بأسانيد صحيحة ]

25/07/2025, 10:53 pm - Alfaaz: Renewal of Iman

اَللّٰهُمَّ جَدِّدِ الْإِيْمَانَ فِيْ قَلْبِيْ

Allāhumma jaddidi-l-īmāna fī qalbī.

O Allah, keep faith rejuvenated in my heart.

ʿAbdullāh b. ʿAmr (radiy Allāhū ‘anhumā) narrates that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: “Indeed, īmān (faith) wears out in your hearts the way a piece of cloth wears out. So ask Allah to rejuvenate īmān (faith) in your hearts.” (Tabrāni, Al-Mu’jam Al-Kabir)

عن عبد اللهِ بن عمرٍو، قال: قال رسولُ اللهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم:إِنَّ الإِيمَانَ لَيَخْلَقُ فِي جَوْفِ أَحَدِكُمْ كَمَا يَخْلَقُ الثَّوْبُ الخَلَقُ؛ فَسَلُوا اللهَ أَنْ يُجَدِّدَ الإِيمَانَ فِي قُلُوبِكُمْ. (المعجم الكبير للطبراني ١٤٦٦٨) <This message was edited>

26/07/2025, 8:01 am - Muzammil New: *_And He it is Who has created the heavens and the earth in six days and His Throne was on the water, that He may try you, which of you is the best in deeds._* [11:7]

ʿAbdullāh bin Masʿūd (may Allah be pleased with him) said:
*Allāh created seven heavens; the span of each one is a journey of five hundred years, and between each one of them five hundred years. And above the seven heavens is the water, and Allāh, may His praise be glorified, is above the Water. Nothing of the deeds of the children of Ādam is hidden from Him. And the earths are seven; between each earth is five hundred years, and the thickness of each earth is five hundred years.*

[Al-Dārimī in al-Radd ʿalā al-Jahmiyyah (33), al-Ṭabarī in al-Tafsīr (23/78), al-Tawḥīd by Ibn Khuzaymah (138, 139 & 598), al-Ṭabarānī (8987), al-Bayhaqī in al-Asmāʾ wa al-Ṣifāt (851), and al-Dhahabī in al-ʿUluww (74); with Ḥasan asānīd]

عن عبدِ اللهِ، قال: خلقَ اللهُ سبعَ سماواتٍ غِلَظُ كلِّ واحدةٍ مسيرةُ ‌خَمْسِمائةِ ‌عامٍ، ‌وبينَ كلِّ واحدةٍ منهنَّ ‌خمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ، وفوقَ السبعِ السماواتِ الماءُ، واللهُ جلَّ ثناؤُه فوقَ الماءِ، لا يَخْفى عليه شيءٌ مِن أعمالِ بني آدمَ. والأرضُ سَبعٌ، ‌بينَ كلِّ أرضٍ ‌خَمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ، وغِلَظُ كلِّ أرضِ ‌خَمسُمائةِ ‌عامٍ

[الدارمي في الرد على الجهمية (٣٣) والطبري في التفسير (٢٣/٧٨) والتوحيد لابن خزيمة (١٣٨ و١٣٩ و598) والطبراني (٨٩٨٧) والبيهقي في الأسماء والصفات (٨٥١) والذهبي في العلو (٧٤) بأسانيد حسنة]

28/07/2025, 7:18 am - Muzammil New: *Prohibition of praying more than 2 before Fajr*
______________________________

Saʿīd bin al-Musayyib looked at a man who was praying after the Adhan for the morning prayer (Fajr), and he prayed excessively. So he (Saʿīd) threw pebbles at him, then said: "If one of you does not know, then let him ask. Indeed, there is no prayer after the Adhan except for two rakʿahs." The man turned away and said: “O Abū Muḥammad, do you fear that Allāh will punish me for praying excessively?” He (Saʿīd) said: *“Rather, I fear that Allāh will punish you for abandoning the Sunnah.”*

[Al-Faqīh wa al-Mutafaqqih (1/381); Isnād Ḥasan]

سَعِيد بْنَ الْمُسَيِّبِ نَظَرَ إِلَى رَجُلٍ صَلَّى بَعْدَ النِّدَاءِ مِنْ صَلَاةِ الصُّبْحِ ، فَأَكْثَرَ الصَّلَاةَ فَحَصَبَهُ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: إِذَا لَمْ يَكُنْ أَحَدُكُمْ يَعْلَمُ فَلْيَسْأَلْ ، إِنَّهُ لَا صَلَاةَ بَعْدَ النِّدَاءِ إِلَّا رَكْعَتَيْنِ قَالَ: فَانْصَرَفَ فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا مُحَمَّدٍ ، أَتَخْشَى أَنْ يُعَذِّبُنِيَ اللَّهُ بِكَثْرَةِ الصَّلَاةِ؟ قَالَ: بَلْ أَخْشَى أَنْ يُعَذِّبَكَ اللَّهُ ‌بِتَرْكِ ‌السُّنَّةِ
[الفقيه والمتفقه (١/٣٨١) وسنده حسن]

29/07/2025, 4:59 pm - Muzammil New: *Do not delay learning*
______________________________

ʿUmar ibn al-Khaṭṭāb (may Allāh be pleased with him) said:
*“Learn before you are appointed (as leaders)”* meaning before you sit before the people (to teach) and are asked (questions).

Abū ʿUbayd al-Qāsim ibn Sallām said: *"(It means) Learn knowledge while you are still young, before you become masters and leaders who are looked upon. For if you do not learn before that, you will feel ashamed to learn it after growing old, and thus you will remain ignorant, taking it (knowledge) from your juniors, and that will bring disgrace upon you."*

[Al-Zuhd by Wakīʿ (102), Ibn Abī Shaybah (27797), al-Dārimī (257), Gharīb al-Ḥadīth by Abū ʿUbayd (635), al-Faqīh wa al-Mutafaqqih (2/153), and al-Madkhal by al-Bayhaqī (373); with Jayyid asānīd]

قال عمر بن الخطاب: تفقهوا قبل ‌أن ‌تسودوا يعني قبل أن تجلسوا للناس فتسألوا

قال أبو عبيد القاسم بن سلام: تعلموا العلم ما دمتم صغاراً قبل أن تصيروا سادةً رؤساء، منظوراً إ ليكم، فإن لم تعلموا قبل ذلك استحييتم أن تعلموه بعد الكبر، فبقيتم جهالاً، تأخذونه من الأصاغر فيزرى ذلك بكم.

[الزهد لوكيع (١٠٢) وابن أبي شيبة (٢٧٧٩٧) والدارمي (٢٥٧) وغريب الحديث لأبي عبيد (٦٣٥) والفقيه والمتفقه من طريق المعدل (٢/١٥٣) والمدخل للبيهقي (٣٧٣) بأسانيد جياد]

______________________________

ʿAbdullāh ibn ʿAmr ibn al-ʿĀṣ (may Allāh be pleased with both) said:
*“The one who plays with dice as gambling is like the eater of pig’s flesh, and the one who plays with them without gambling is like one who dips his hand into the blood of a pig.”*

[Al-Adab al-Mufrad (1277) and Dhamm al-Malāhī by Ibn Abī al-Dunyā (77); Ḥasan asānīd]

Alī ibn Abi Talib (radiallahu anhu) said:

"The best of your women is she who is

| pleasant in scent || excellent in cooking |

when she spends she does so moderately, and when she withholds, she does so wisely.

She is among the workers of Allah, and the worker of Allah is never disappointed."

Bahjat al-Majālis by Ibn 'Abd al-Barr pp. 33-34

30/07/2025, 10:21 pm - +971 50 518 3779: السلام عليكم ورحمة الله وبركاته 
أحسن الله اليكم


Is this authentic? And if not, is there any different narrations where it is:

حَدَّثَنَا بِذَلِكَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدَةَ الضَّبِّيُّ ، قَالَ : حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ ، وَالْمُعْتَمِرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ ، قَالَا : حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ - وَهُوَ قَهْرَمَانُ آلِ الزُّبَيْرِ - عَنْ سَالِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ ، عَنْ جَدِّهِ أَنَّ **رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ قَالَ : مَنْ قَالَ فِي السُّوقِ : " لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ يُحْيِي وَيُمِيتُ وَهُوَ حَيٌّ لَا يَمُوتُ بِيَدِهِ الْخَيْرُ وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ، كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لَهُ أَلْفَ أَلْفِ حَسَنَةٍ، وَمَحَا عَنْهُ أَلْفَ أَلْفِ سَيِّئَةٍ، وَبَنَى لَهُ بَيْتًا فِي الْجَنَّة ". **
وَعَمْرُو بْنُ دِينَارٍ هَذَا هُوَ شَيْخٌ بَصْرِيٌّ، وَقَدْ تَكَلَّمَ فِيهِ بَعْضُ أَصْحَابِ الْحَدِيثِ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، وَرَوَاهُ يَحْيَى بْنُ سُلَيْمٍ الطَّائِفِيُّ، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ، وَلَمْ يَذْكُرْ فِيهِ عَنْ عُمَرَ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ.

Tirmidhi 3429

30/07/2025, 10:37 pm - +971 50 518 3779: جزاكم الله خيرا
30/07/2025, 11:14 pm - محمد عبد الوهاب: قال الإمام عبد الله بن عبد الرحمن الدارمي رحمه الله في "سننه" (210) :
أَخْبَرَنَا الْحَكَمُ بْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ ، أَنبَأَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ يَحْيَى ، قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبِي ، يُحَدِّثُ ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: " كُنَّا نَجْلِسُ عَلَى بَابِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ ، قَبْلَ صَلَاةِ الْغَدَاةِ ، فَإِذَا خَرَجَ ، مَشَيْنَا مَعَهُ إِلَى الْمَسْجِدِ ، فَجَاءَنَا أَبُو مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيُّ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ فَقَالَ: أَخَرَجَ إِلَيْكُمْ أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ ؟ قُلْنَا: لَا، بَعْدُ ، فَجَلَسَ مَعَنَا حَتَّى خَرَجَ ، فَلَمَّا خَرَجَ، قُمْنَا إِلَيْهِ جَمِيعًا، فَقَالَ لَهُ أَبُو مُوسَى: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، إِنِّي رَأَيْتُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ آنِفًا أَمْرًا أَنْكَرْتُهُ وَلَمْ أَرَ - وَالْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ - إِلَّا خَيْرًا ، قَالَ: فَمَا هُوَ؟ فَقَالَ: إِنْ عِشْتَ فَسَتَرَاهُ ، قَالَ: رَأَيْتُ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ قَوْمًا حِلَقًا جُلُوسًا يَنْتَظِرُونَ الصَّلَاةَ فِي كُلِّ حَلْقَةٍ رَجُلٌ، وَفِي أَيْدِيهِمْ حصًا، فَيَقُولُ: كَبِّرُوا مِائَةً ، فَيُكَبِّرُونَ مِائَةً، فَيَقُولُ: هَلِّلُوا مِائَةً، فَيُهَلِّلُونَ مِائَةً ، وَيَقُولُ: سَبِّحُوا مِائَةً، فَيُسَبِّحُونَ مِائَةً ، قَالَ: فَمَاذَا قُلْتَ لَهُمْ ؟ ، قَالَ: مَا قُلْتُ لَهُمْ شَيْئًا انْتِظَارَ رَأْيِكَ أَوِ انْتظارَ أَمْرِكَ ، قَالَ : " أَفَلَا أَمَرْتَهُمْ أَنْ يَعُدُّوا سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ ، وَضَمِنْتَ لَهُمْ أَنْ لَا يَضِيعَ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِهِمْ " ، ثُمَّ مَضَى وَمَضَيْنَا مَعَهُ حَتَّى أَتَى حَلْقَةً مِنْ تِلْكَ الْحِلَقِ، فَوَقَفَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَقَالَ: " مَا هَذَا الَّذِي أَرَاكُمْ تَصْنَعُونَ؟ " قَالُوا: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ حصًا نَعُدُّ بِهِ التَّكْبِيرَ وَالتَّهْلِيلَ وَالتَّسْبِيحَ ، قَالَ: " فَعُدُّوا سَيِّئَاتِكُمْ ، فَأَنَا ضَامِنٌ أَنْ لَا يَضِيعَ مِنْ حَسَنَاتِكُمْ شَيْءٌ ، وَيْحَكُمْ يَا أُمَّةَ مُحَمَّدٍ ، مَا أَسْرَعَ هَلَكَتَكُمْ هَؤُلَاءِ صَحَابَةُ نَبِيِّكُمْ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ مُتَوَافِرُونَ ، وَهَذِهِ ثِيَابُهُ لَمْ تَبْلَ ، وَآنِيَتُهُ لَمْ تُكْسَرْ، وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّكُمْ لَعَلَى مِلَّةٍ هِيَ أَهْدَى مِنْ مِلَّةِ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ أوْ مُفْتَتِحُو بَابِ ضَلَالَةٍ " ، قَالُوا: وَاللَّهِ يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، مَا أَرَدْنَا إِلَّا الْخَيْرَ. قَالَ: " وَكَمْ مِنْ مُرِيدٍ لِلْخَيْرِ لَنْ يُصِيبَهُ ، إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ حَدَّثَنَا أَنَّ قَوْمًا يَقْرَءُونَ الْقُرْآنَ لَا يُجَاوِزُ تَرَاقِيَهُمْ ، وَايْمُ اللَّهِ مَا أَدْرِي لَعَلَّ أَكْثَرَهُمْ مِنْكُمْ " ثُمَّ تَوَلَّى عَنْهُمْ ، فَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ سَلَمَةَ: رَأَيْنَا عَامَّةَ أُولَئِكَ الْحِلَقِ يُطَاعِنُونَا يَوْمَ النَّهْرَوَانِ مَعَ الْخَوَارِجِ " .
وهكذا رواه بحشل في "تاريخ واسط" (ص 198) من طريق عُمَرو بْن يَحْيَى بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ سَلَمَةَ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ، قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، قَالَ: " كُنَّا جُلُوسًا عَلَى بَابِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ ... فذكره
